class=\"post-28 page type-page status-publish hentry entry\">\n\n\t\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\">Be a Converterlator!</h1> \n\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<h2>What are you doing with your time, talent and treasure?</h2>\n<p>Have you shifted the gears of your life from park into drive? Each day provides new opportunities for us to serve God by strategically using the resources he has entrusted to us.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://kingdomnomics.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Park-to-Drive.jpg\" class=\"fbx-link fbx-instance\"><img class=\"alignright size-medium wp-image-2290\" src=\"http://kingdomnomics.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Park-to-Drive-300x300.jpg\" alt=\"Shift the gears of your life from park to drive\" width=\"300\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://kingdomnomics.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Park-to-Drive-300x300.jpg 300w, https://kingdomnomics.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Park-to-Drive-150x150.jpg 150w, https://kingdomnomics.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Park-to-Drive.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\"></a>The message contained on this website will only make sense for the person who has a <a href=\"http://kingdomnomics.com/begin-the-relationship/\" target=\"_blank\">relationship with God</a> through Jesus Christ alone. It is important to understand that what we do (our works) in this world after we come to know Christ, impacts how we will live in the world to come. Christ not only came into this world to change where we will spend our eternal destiny, which is achieved when we put our trust in him as our personal Lord and Savior, but how we will spend eternity, which is impacted by what we do with the resources he has made available to us.</p>\n<p>The Bible is our guide in how we should not only live our lives here on earth, using our time, talent, and treasure for God’s glory, but also how we should prepare for entering the world that will last forever.</p>\n<p>A Converterlator is an agent of change; a transformer who not only experiences a life of joy now, but who also makes decisions that will echo into eternity. As I have used my time, talent, and treasure for God’s kingdom, I have experienced a life of excitement, opportunity, impact, and what I know is going to be a legacy.</p>\n<p>As you read the articles on this website, you can experience the same thing! Take your life “from park to drive” and let your life echo into eternity.</p>\n<p>Phil</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"></p><div style=\"clear:both;width:100%;float:none;\"><a class=\"read-button\" href=\"/from-convert-to-converterlator/\">Find out more</a></div>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n\t\t</div><!-- end .entry-content -->\n\t\t\n\t</div><!-- end .postclass -->\n\t<div id=\"home-recent-posts\">\n    <div class=\"wrap\"><div class=\"home-recent-posts widget-area\"><div id=\"featured-post-2\" class=\"widget featuredpost\"><div class=\"widget-wrap\"><h4 class=\"widgettitle\">Recent Posts</h4>\n<div class=\"post-3480 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-reflections-of-a-kingdom-boy tag-blessings tag-devotional tag-psalm-443 tag-source-of-live entry\"><h2><a href=\"https://kingdomnomics.com/glory-belongs-to-god/\" title=\"Glory Belongs to God\">Glory Belongs to God</a></h2><p>Scripture: Psalm 44:3, NKJV\n“For they did not gain possession of the land by their own sword, nor did their own arm save them; but it was Your right hand, Your arm, and the light of Your countenance, because You favored them.” (Psalm 44:3 NKJV)\n\nFrom a human perspective it is difficult for us … <a href=\"https://kingdomnomics.com/glory-belongs-to-god/\" class=\"more-link\">Read More...</a></p></div><!--end post_class()-->\n\n<div class=\"post-3475 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-reflections-of-a-kingdom-boy tag-dead-to-sin tag-devotional tag-holy-spirit tag-relationship-with-god tag-romans-611 entry\"><h2><a href=\"https://kingdomnomics.com/relationship-key-to-fruitful-life/\" title=\"Relationship: The Key Component to a Fruitful Life\">Relationship: The Key Component to a Fruitful Life</a></h2><p>Scripture: Romans 6:11, NLT\n“So you also should consider yourselves to be dead to the power of sin and alive to God through Christ Jesus.” (Romans 6:11, NLT)\n\nThis is an incredible statement to be making to the believer in Jesus Christ. A Converterlator is an agent of change; a transformer who not only experiences a life of joy now, but who also makes decisions that will echo into eternity.</p>\n<p>The Bible is clear that we will experience rewards in heaven. For those who take seriously the coming of a new life–one that follows earthly life–nothing could be more important.</p></td>\n</tr>\n</tbody>\n</table>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<div style=\"text-align:
